## <a id="prompt-2004239718121161200">å¾¡å¥½çƒ§ï¼šå¤å¤é£Ÿè°±ä¸­çš„ç¾å‘³ç»†èŠ‚</a> (<a href="https://x.com/Gdgtify/status/2004239718121161201" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Gadgetify</a>)

```
Input: Okonomiyaki
 
Analysis: Extract key ingredients, cooking techniques, and cultural food elements
Goal: A cookbook where ingredients and dishes emerge in delicious detail
Rules:

```

```
è¾“å…¥ï¼šå¾¡å¥½çƒ§

åˆ†æï¼šæå–å…³é”®é£Ÿæã€çƒ¹é¥ªæŠ€æœ¯åŠæ–‡åŒ–é£Ÿå“å…ƒç´ 
ç›®æ ‡ï¼šä¸€æœ¬é£Ÿè°±ï¼Œå…¶ä¸­é£Ÿæå’Œèœè‚´ä»¥ç¾å‘³çš„ç»†èŠ‚å‘ˆç°

## <a id="prompt-2004036691879743700">åœ£è¯ç¾é£ŸåŒé¢æµ·æŠ¥</a> (<a href="https://x.com/icreatelife/status/2004036691879743733" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Kris Kashtanova</a>)

<img src="../..//images/2025-12-25/2004036691879743700_0.jpg" alt="åœ£è¯ç¾é£ŸåŒé¢æµ·æŠ¥">

```
Clean contemporary square culinary poster featuring [FOOD_ITEM] against a flat [BACKGROUND_COLOR] backdrop. A razor-sharp vertical white divider cuts directly down the middle of the composition, separating the primary subject into equal portions. The first half displays a hyper-realistic photograph of the main dish with authentic surface details, true-to-life coloring, and natural illumination, precisely trimmed at the midpoint divider. The second half transforms into a minimal outline illustration that mirrors the identical shape and key features of the photographed side, keeping consistent scale and viewing angle. Surrounding the illustrated portion, scatter whimsical white sketched elements and casual handwritten-style typography stating â€œ[LABEL_TEXT]â€ using matching line thicknessâ€”incorporate directional pointers, dynamic streaks, and basic component graphics tied to the dish. Generous blank space throughout, uniform background tone, balanced diffused studio brightness, minimal shadow presence, contemporary commercial design style, human-free, object-focused composition.
```

## <a id="prompt-2004601351146532900">ç§‘å­¦å®¶çš„å¾®ç¼©å¯¹å†³</a> (<a href="https://x.com/Gdgtify/status/2004601351146532917" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Gadgetify</a>)

<img src="../..//images/2025-12-26/2004601351146532900_0.jpg" alt="ç§‘å­¦å®¶çš„å¾®ç¼©å¯¹å†³">

```
Do this for Einstein and a competitor of his 


 Invention = [User Choice, e.g., Electricity, The Airplane, The Telephone]

Phase 1: Historical Conflict Analysis
1.  Identify Rivals: Determine the two main historical figures associated with this invention (e.g., Tesla vs. Edison, Wright Bros vs. Curtiss).
2.  Identify The Tech: Distinguish their competing methods (e.g., AC Coils vs. DC Bulbs).
3.  Identify The Era: Select appropriate "Giant" background clutter (e.g., Victorian newspapers, 1920s fountain pens).

Phase 2: Visual Execution
Goal: A "Macro Diorama" of a Rivalry. A messy, highly detailed flat-lay of a shared historical workspace where the two rivals exist as tiny living figurines battling over their creation.

Rules:
The Stage: A large, yellowed Patent Diagram or Blueprint lies flat on a wooden desk. The paper is wrinkled and covered in scribbled corrections.

The Tiny Rivals: Two hyper-realistic miniature figurines (Inventor A and Rival B) are standing on opposite sides of the document. They are positioned at their own tiny wooden desks or workstations on top of the paper.

The Conflict: They are gesturing aggressively at each other. The Invention itself is physically emerging from the center of the paper between them (e.g., a glowing 3D lightbulb or a spinning biplane propeller), acting as the barrier or prize they are fighting over.

The "Giant" Terrain (Surroundings): The scene is surrounded by massive, period-accurate objects acting as a landscape:

A "Giant" wall of newspapers with headlines about their legal battles.
 Massive burnt fuses or broken prototypes scattered like boulders.
 A spilled cup of coffee creating a "lake" near one of the figures.
  Giant tools (calipers, screwdrivers) casting long shadows.
Perspective: Slightly angled 45-degree macro shot looking down at the patent.
Texture: Dust motes, scratched mahogany wood, paper grain, metallic reflections.
Lighting: Cinematic Macro Lighting. A warm desk lamp illuminates the scene, but the Invention in the center emits its own light (e.g., blue electrical arcs vs. yellow filament glow), lighting the faces of the tiny figures.

Output: ONE image, 4:5 aspect ratio, photorealistic historical macro photography, tilt-shift effect.

```

Urban Modern â€” Dark espresso hardwood, charcoal textured walls, sleek white Italian leather seating, chrome and glass surfaces, large-scale black and white photography, geometric black/white/gray rugs, layered sheer and blackout curtains. Palette: charcoal, white, chrome, black, cool gray. Lighting: layered recessed and LED strips, dramatic. Mood: sophisticated, city penthouse, nightlife elegance.

Row 3 â€“ Global & Cultural:

Japanese Zen â€” Tatami-style natural flooring, off-white lime-washed walls, low platform seating in charcoal linen, shoji screen dividers, bonsai on simple stands, calligraphy scroll art, floor cushions, black iron teapot, rice paper window panels. Palette: off-white, charcoal, bamboo, black, moss green. Lighting: soft diffused, contemplative. Mood: meditative, balanced, wabi-sabi beauty.
Moroccan Bohemian â€” Terra-cotta geometric zellige tile, warm textured stucco walls, low carved wooden seating with jewel-tone cushions, brass lantern pendants, ornate wooden screens, embroidered leather poufs, bone inlay mirrors, layered vintage rugs. Palette: terra-cotta, sapphire, ruby, gold, turquoise. Lighting: lanterns casting patterned shadows. Mood: exotic, layered, sensory richness.
Mediterranean Coastal â€” Tumbled limestone flooring, white textured plaster walls with arched niches, deep natural white linen seating, driftwood surfaces, terracotta pots with olive branches, iron candelabras, billowing white gauze curtains, blue/white ceramics, seagrass rugs. Palette: white, terracotta, Mediterranean blue, olive green. Lighting: bright sun-drenched, golden. Mood: relaxed, sun-kissed, Aegean escape.
Indian Maximalist â€” Inlaid marble flooring, deep peacock blue walls, ornate carved wooden seating with silk cushions in marigold and fuchsia, brass figurines, embroidered floor bolsters, carved jali screens, hanging brass bells, marigold garlands, gold-embroidered silk curtains. Palette: peacock blue, marigold, fuchsia, gold. Lighting: rich warm brass lamp glow. Mood: opulent, celebratory, sensory abundance.

Row 4 â€“ Specialty & Emerging:

Art Deco Revival â€” High-gloss black lacquered flooring, deep navy walls with geometric gold molding, curved emerald velvet seating, sunburst brass mirrors, stepped geometric shelving, marble and brass accents, frosted glass sculptural lamps, gold velvet drapes with black trim. Palette: emerald, navy, gold, black, marble. Lighting: glamorous wall sconces, dramatic. Mood: lavish, theatrical, 1920s grandeur.
Biophilic Modern â€” Light cork flooring, living moss wall installation, organic-shaped sage green bouclÃ© seating, natural edge wood surfaces, hanging planters at multiple heights, terrariums, stone pebble accents, abundant air-purifying plants, undyed natural linen curtains. Palette: every green shade, natural wood, stone gray, cork. Lighting: greenhouse-like, supplemental grow lights. Mood: alive, oxygen-rich, nature immersion.
Japandi Fusion â€” Light ash flooring, warm white walls with single black accent stripe, low streamlined warm gray wool seating, pale wood with black metal frame surfaces, single large ceramic vessel, paper pendant lights, bonsai, ikebana arrangements, warm beige linen curtains. Palette: warm white, ash, black accent, pale wood, sage. Lighting: bright but soft, material-focused. Mood: refined simplicity, warm minimalism.
Avant-Garde Maximalist â€” Checkered black/white marble flooring, colorful Memphis-style geometric wall patterns, curved hot pink velvet seating, wavy asymmetrical mirrors, abstract sculptural lighting, clashing patterns throughout, salon-style art collection, neon sign art, mixed metals. Palette: hot pink, electric blue, yellow, black, white. Lighting: theatrical, neon accents, spotlighting. Mood: bold, rule-breaking, creative chaos.

Post-processing: individual color grading per style mood. Output: high-resolution architectural portfolio quality. Full spectrum from serene minimalism to opulent maximalism

## <a id="prompt-2005233594130973000">ç°ä»£é£æ ¼çš„è¶…å†™å®ç¾é£Ÿæ‘„å½±</a> (<a href="https://x.com/aleenaamiir/status/2005233594130972845" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Aleena Amir</a>)

```
Fashion catalog layout design in magazine style. Clean white background with professional typography.

Top header: "Adidas" on left (light gray italic), "JERLIN" center (bold black), "Autumn 2026" on right (light gray italic)

Main layout composition:

Right side (three smaller images stacked vertically):
- Top image: Close-up detail of jacket chest and sleeve area showing [JACKET_DESIGN] and triple stripes.
- Middle image: Full body shot, standing straight, showing complete outfit from head to toe.
- Bottom image: Back view showing the back [JACKET_DESIGN] design of the jacket.

Bottom text area:
Large bold headline: "AUTUMN'S GOLDEN HOUR." (black, sans-serif font)
Subtitle below: "A fusion of heritage details and modern ease." (smaller, gray text)

Professional fashion photography style, minimalist composition, soft even lighting, editorial quality, clean aesthetic, proper spacing and margins. IMPORTANT: Maintain exact facial features, hairstyle, and glasses from reference photo.

```

å³ä¾§ï¼ˆä¸‰ä¸ªè¾ƒå°çš„å›¾åƒå‚ç›´æ’åˆ—ï¼‰ï¼š
- é¡¶éƒ¨å›¾ç‰‡ï¼šå¤¹å…‹èƒ¸éƒ¨å’Œè¢–å­åŒºåŸŸçš„ç‰¹å†™ç»†èŠ‚ï¼Œæ˜¾ç¤ºã€å¤¹å…‹è®¾è®¡ã€‘å’Œä¸‰æ¡çº¹ã€‚

## <a id="prompt-2005097871977447736">å…ƒæ—¦ç‰¹è¾‘-å¤å¤æ——è¢ååª›é£</a> (<a href="https://x.com/songguoxiansen/status/2005097871977447736" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">æ¾æœå…ˆæ£®</a>)

```

Starbucks Iced Caramel Macchiato
A surreal advertising photomontage of a Starbucks-style Iced Caramel Macchiato plastic cup acting as a snow-capped mountain peak. Gourmet Double Cheeseburger
A hyper-realistic food manipulation piece centered on a massive gourmet double cheeseburger. The burger acts as an erupting volcano; molten cheddar cheese flows like lava down cascades of beef patties. Strawberry Cheesecake Ice Cream Cone

Honey & Nut Crunch

The thick stream of honey is defying gravity, swirling around the dipper like ribbons of liquid amber glass and golden silk fabric. Raw almonds and oat clusters are suspended in the air around the honey flow. Soft, warm backlighting creating a glowing, angelic atmosphere. Ultra-detailed sticky texture. No text, purely organic and elegant.

## <a id="prompt-2005670356745322800">æç®€é£æ ¼å“ç‰Œé¦–å­—æ¯å•ä½“å¾½æ ‡è®¾è®¡</a> (<a href="https://x.com/AmirMushich/status/2005670356745322759" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">AmirMuÅ¡iÄ‡</a>)

<img src="../..//images/2025-12-29/2005670356745322800_0.jpg" alt="æç®€é£æ ¼å“ç‰Œé¦–å­—æ¯å•ä½“å¾½æ ‡è®¾è®¡">

```
A flat, minimalist vector design featuring a highly stylized single letter monogram with the official brand logo below it, representing [BRAND NAME].

**MAIN ELEMENT (THE MONOGRAM):**
The center of the design features ONLY the single first letter of "[BRAND NAME]". The style is "Ornamental Vector Typography" with high calligraphic artistry, mimicking bespoke luxury monograms. This is not a standard font; it is a Highly customized, artistic glyph with elegant flourishes, exaggerated swashes, or ornamental serifs. The lines are clean, precise, and perfectly smooth vector graphics.

**SECONDARY ELEMENT (BRAND IDENTIFIER):**
Directly below the main stylized letter, positioned centrally, include the actual, original official logomark or logotype of "[BRAND NAME]". This element must be rendered significantly smaller than the main letter above it.

**FINISH & TEXTURE (STRICT):**
Absolutely zero texture, zero embossing, zero shadows, and zero gradients anywhere in the image. It must look like a perfectly flat digital illustration or screen print.

**COLOR PALETTE (AI-DRIVEN & HIGH CONTRAST):**
1.  **Background:** A single, solid, flat color block chosen by the AI to represent the vibe of [BRAND NAME].
2.  **Main Monogram Color:** A single, solid, flat color that creates a sharp, high contrast against the background.
3.  **Secondary Logo Color:** The small official logo below must be monochrome. It must be EITHER solid white OR solid dark grayâ€”chosen automatically based on whichever offers the best readability against the chosen background color.
```

## <a id="prompt-2007497261492920800">å¥¢åæœ¨è´¨é¦™è°ƒé¦™æ°´AUREN</a> (<a href="https://x.com/SiboEsenkova/status/2007497261492920739" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Sibo Esenkova</a>)

<img src="../..//images/2026-01-03/2007497261492920800_0.jpg" alt="å¥¢åæœ¨è´¨é¦™è°ƒé¦™æ°´AUREN">

<img src="../..//images/2026-01-03/2007497261492920800_2.jpg" alt="å¥¢åæœ¨è´¨é¦™è°ƒé¦™æ°´AUREN">

```
Ultra high-end fragrance campaign photography for a luxury unisex woody perfume brand, created for a premium e-commerce category card.

A clearly recognizable luxury perfume bottle.
Elegant cylindrical or softly rectangular glass bottle.
Thick crystal-clear glass with slight warm tint.
Visible amber-to-light-wood toned liquid.
Premium atomizer and spray neck.
Heavy matte or brushed wood-toned cap with subtle metallic core.

Front label:
Minimal luxury label.
Fake brand name: â€œAURENâ€.
Refined serif or modern high-fashion typography.
Centered placement.
Muted warm beige or soft taupe label tone.
Subtle embossed or hot-stamped details.
Clearly readable, unmistakably perfume.

Scene:
Warm woody-inspired luxury still life.
Natural wood elements used with restraint.
Smooth walnut or oak wood block surface.
Soft bark textures, clean wood grain.
Optional single element of dry branch or shaved wood curl.
No clutter, no rustic mess.
Feels calm, grounded, expensive.

Lighting:
Warm, skin-like studio lighting.
Soft directional light mimicking late afternoon sun.
Light passes through glass and liquid, creating depth.
Subtle shadow gradients.
No harsh highlights.
No cold reflections.

Camera:
Shot by a world-class luxury fragrance photography team.
Medium format camera (Hasselblad / Phase One).
85mm lens.
Shallow depth of field.
Perfect focus on bottle, label, glass thickness.
Natural optical falloff.

Mood & Style:
Woody.
Warm.
Grounded.
Human.
Genderless.
Quiet confidence.
Feels like warm skin, clean wood, soft leather.
Luxury designer fragrance, not home scent, not candle.

Framing:
Vertical composition for category card.
Bottle as clear hero.
Wood elements framing subtly.
Clean negative space preserved.
Instant perfume recognition at first glance.

Quality:
Hyper-realistic.
True photography look.
No CGI.
No artificial glow.
No watermark.
No extra text.
Feels like a high-budget global fragrance launch.
```

## <a id="prompt-2007535691157143600">æç®€é»‘ç™½çŸ¢é‡è‚–åƒæ’ç”»</a> (<a href="https://x.com/AmirMushich/status/2007535691157143563" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">AmirMuÅ¡iÄ‡</a>)

<img src="../..//images/2026-01-03/2007535691157143600_0.jpg" alt="æç®€é»‘ç™½çŸ¢é‡è‚–åƒæ’ç”»">

```
A minimalist, black-and-white flat vector illustration portrait of [CHARACTER NAME], rendered in the expressive "Notion avatar" art style.

LINE WORK & VIBE:

Style: Use THICK, UNIFORM black outlines (monoline weight). The lines should feel organic, smooth, and confident, not rigidly geometric or robotic like generic icons.

Vibe: The character should have a distinct personality and a relaxed, cool, or friendly expression. Focus on stylized features, unique hairstyles, and defining accessories to convey character.

SELECTIVE BLACK FILLS (CRITICAL):

Unlike pure outline icons, utilize Solid Black Fills selectively and strategically.

Where to Fill: Use solid black for prominent hair masses, beards, eyebrows, sunglasses, or dark clothing elements.

Where to Keep White: The skin, main face area, and lighter elements must remain pure flat white inside the thick outlines.

COMPOSITION & TECHNICAL:

No shading, no gray tones, no gradients. Only pure Black and pure White.

Clean bust or headshot composition centered on a white background.

High contrast, clean 2D vector graphics.
```

## <a id="prompt-2007722721967321000">è¶…å†™å®ç”µå½±æ„Ÿåœ°ä¸‹èµ›è½¦æµ·æŠ¥</a> (<a href="https://x.com/harboriis/status/2007722721967321132" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Harboriis</a>)

<img src="../..//images/2026-01-04/2007722721967321000_0.jpg" alt="è¶…å†™å®ç”µå½±æ„Ÿåœ°ä¸‹èµ›è½¦æµ·æŠ¥">

```
Ultra-realistic cinematic underground racing poster, with a dark, smoky and intense atmosphere inspired by nighttime street-race culture.

Create a triple-layer composition:

Foreground Scene (Full-body)

A dramatic full-body shot of the man standing in the middle of an abandoned industri-al road at night. He should be holding a racing helmet under one arm and standing confidently beside a modified street-race car drifting in slow motion behind him, gen-erating heavy smoke, sparks, and tire marks. The ground must reflect light from the car's headlights, adding wet-asphalt cinematic reflections.

Clothing: black jacket (leather or tactical), dark pants, rings and accessories, subtle metallic reflections, realistic fabric texture with shadows and folds.

Mid-layer Portrait

A medium-sized portrait of the man, facing sideways with a stern, focused expression, as if preparing for a race or confrontation. Add subtle fog around the edges and soft rim lighting from the streetlights above. The portrait must blend smoothly with the drifting smoke from the car.

Hero Background Portrait (Large Face)

A massive intense close-up of the man's face dominating the top of the poster, ex-pression strong and fearless. Add faint reflections of racing lights in the sunglasses and a subtle speedometer graphic overlay behind him. Smoke and moonlight should frame this portrait, creating a dramatic halo effect.

Atmosphere and Effects:

Dark palette with blacks, grays, metallic silver and moon-blue.

Minimal neon, no colorful beams.

Mist, drifting smoke, sparks from asphalt.

A blurred checkered-flag motion effect behind the background portrait.

Soft city skyline silhouette far behind the smoke.

Car:

A completely different model from the previous prompt: Nissan GT-R Black Edition (or similar JDM icon), hyper-detailed with glossy reflections, racing decals, visible car-bon-fiber textures, and headlights slicing through fog.

Face Replacement Instruction:

Replace all faces with the face from the photo I will upload. Keep lighting, expression, angle, texture and realism consistent with the cinematic scene. Do not alter the per-son's natural facial features. Blend the face perfectly into the poster.

Final Rendering Style:

8K resolution, ultra-sharp details, premium Hollywood poster composition, dramatic depth of field, misty environment, crisp reflections, slight vignette, full photorealism.
```

```

A striking, conceptual advertisement for Rolex, featuring a luxury wristwatch as the central hero element. The scene uses a bold visual metaphor to represent precision and reliability. ## <a id="prompt-2007122463151534300">æ€€æ—§æ¸¸æˆå¡å¸¦å†…çš„å¾®ç¼©ä¸–ç•Œ</a> (<a href="https://x.com/Gdgtify/status/2007122463151534322" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Gadgetify</a>)

```
Input: Legend of Zelda:   Role:  Gaming Historian & Memory Card Sculptor

 Input:  [Video Game, e.g., The Legend of Zelda]

 Phase 1: Game DNA Analysis 
1. Identify core gameplay loop (exploration-puzzle-boss / die-learn-overcome)
2. Select 4 hidden gem games (indie or cult classics)  and their Release Years .
3. Extract 3 iconic in-game items and the game's signature color palette

 Phase 2: Visual Execution 
 Goal:  2x2 Grid of "Opened Game Cartridges as World Containers"

 Rules per Panel: 
-  The Shell:  A cracked-open retro game cartridge (NES, Genesis, PS1 case)  with the Game's Title clearly printed on the top spine label. 
-  The Circuitboard:  The internal PCB becomes a miniature topographical game map
-  The World:  Key game locations built in 3D on the circuit board (castle, dungeon, boss arena)
-  The Hero:  Tiny pixel-art-style figurine of the protagonist mid-action
-  The Enemies:  2-3 micro-enemy models positioned as threats
-  The HUD:   A floating holographic UI element displays the text: "[Game Name] | [Year]" in a retro font. 
-  The Manual:  Weathered instruction booklet page visible underneath showing retro game art
-  The Atmosphere:  CRT scan-line effect overlaid, nostalgic warm glow

 Output:  2x2 Grid, Nostalgic Product Photography, soft focus on edges
```
